   <script>
    function loadCSS( href, before, media ){
     "use strict";
 		var doc = window.document;
 		var ss = doc.createElement( "link" );
 		var ref;
 		if( before ){
 			ref = before;
 		}
 		else {
 			var refs = ( doc.body || doc.getElementsByTagName( "head" )[ 0 ] ).childNodes;
 			ref = refs[ refs.length - 1];
 		}
 		var sheets = doc.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore( ss, ( before ? ref : ref.nextSibling ) );
 		var onloadcssdefined = function( cb ){
 			var resolvedHref = ss.href;
 			var i = sheets.length;
 			while( i-- ){
 				if( sheets[ i ].href === resolvedHref ){
 					return cb();
 				}
 			}
 			setTimeout(function() {
 				onloadcssdefined( cb );
 			});
 		};
 		ss.onloadcssdefined = onloadcssdefined;
 		onloadcssdefined(function() {
 			ss.media = media || "all";
 		});
 		return ss;
 	};

       var basketdb = { "dataSku": [], "dataPrice": [], "dataNo": [] };
       localStorage.setItem( "basketCache", JSON.stringify(basketdb) );
       var jsondb = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("dataCache"));
       var categoriesStr = "";
       jsondb.forEach(function(element){
         categoriesStr = element.cats + ", " + element.subcats;
         element.categories = categoriesStr;
       });
       var productsStr = "";
       var basketsStr = "";
       var brick0 = '</td></tr>';
       var brick1 = '</td><td><button class="btn btn-success basket" data-basket="';
       var brick2 = '"><i class="fa fa-cart-arrow-down"></i></button></td></tr>';
       var trd = '</td><td class="test-center product-sku-list">';
       var priceArray = [];
       var produkt2basket = '';
       var info = [];
       jsondb.forEach(function(element){
         productsStr = "";
         basketsStr = "";
         info = element.infos;
         info.forEach(function(el,index){
           if (element.instock[index] > 0) {
           priceArray = el.bulkprice[0].toString().split(".");
           if (priceArray.length == 2) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + "," + priceArray[1]}
           if (priceArray.length == 2 && priceArray[1].length == 1) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + "," + priceArray[1] + "0"}
           if (priceArray.length == 1) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + ",00"}
           produkt2basket = element.sku + el.subsku;
           productsStr += '<tr><td class="test-center product-sku-list">' + el.skucat1 + trd +  el.skucat2 + trd + element.sku + el.subsku + trd + priceFormat + brick1 + produkt2basket + brick2;
           basketsStr += '<tr><td class="test-center product-sku-list" data-basket="' + produkt2basket + '">' + el.skucat1 + trd +  el.skucat2 + trd + element.sku + el.subsku + trd + priceFormat + brick0;
           }
         });
         element.products = productsStr;
         element.baskets = basketsStr;
       });
       localStorage.setItem( "dataCache", JSON.stringify(jsondb) );
     } catch (e) {
       alert('Eine Version ohne lokale Datenbank gibt es bald.');
     }

   <script id="bridgeland-basket-template" type="text/template">
    <% _.each( productList.listVals, function( listVal ){ %>
       <% var index = _.findIndex( productList.listVals, function(str){ return str == listVal; }); %>
       <% var pointer = productList.listPointers[index]; %>
       <% var listItem = productList.listItems[pointer]; %>
       <% var listNo = productList.listNos[pointer]; %>
       <% var iPointer = productList.listIPointers[index]; %>
       <% var listIPrice = listItem.price[iPointer]; %>
       <% var listPrice = listIPrice * listNo; %>
       <%  var priceFormat = "?"; %>
       <%  var priceArray = listPrice.toString().split("."); %>
       <%  if (priceArray.length == 2) { %>
         <%  if (priceArray[1].length == 2) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + "," + priceArray[1]} %>
         <%  if (priceArray[1].length != 0 && priceArray[1].length == 1) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + "," + priceArray[1] + "0"} %>
       <%  } %>
       <%  if (priceArray.length == 1) { priceFormat = priceArray[0] + ",00"} %>
       <div class="col-xs-12" data-basketListItemSku="<%= listVal %>" style="margin-left:0;margin-right:0;padding:0;">
         <div class="card" style="margin-left:0;margin-right:0;">
           <div class="card-block" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="false" style="padding: 0;">
             <table>
               <tr><td class="basket-product">
                 <div class="shop-bridgeland-<%= listItem.skuID %>" style="border: solid 1px #ffcc66;"></div>
               </td><td>
                 <div class="test-narrow" style="margin-left:2px;">
                   <div class="product-name-list"><%- listItem.name %></div>
                   <div class="product-details-list boxed-horizontal">
                     <div class="test-center product-sku-list" style="flex: 0 1 auto;"><%- listItem.sku %></div>
                     <span class="btn btn-danger label delete-basket-item" style="line-height: 1.5em">X</span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="boxed-horizontal-basket">
                     <div class="product-sku-list" style="display: flex;align-items: center;justify-content: center;"><%= listVal %></div>
                     <form class="form-inline">
                       <input type="number" class="form-control basket-product-number" placeholder="" value="<%= listNo %>" min="1" max="99">
                     </form>
                     <div class="product-price-list" style="display: flex;align-items: center;justify-content: center;"><%= priceFormat %>&euro;</div>
                   </div>
                 </div>
               </td></tr>
             </table>
           </div>
           <div class="collapse">
             <div class="card-block" style="padding: 0;">
               <!-- Tab panes init -->
               <ul class="nav nav-tabs" role="tablist">
                 <li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link active" href="#" data-target="#basket-products-<%= listItem.skuID %>" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">Bestellen</a></li>
                 <li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="#" data-target="#basket-text-<%= listItem.skuID %>" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">Text</a></li>
                 <li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="#" data-target="#basket-picture-<%= listItem.skuID %>" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">Bild</a></li>
               </ul>
               <!-- Tab panes -->
               <div class="tab-content">
                 <div class="tab-pane active" id="basket-products-<%= listItem.skuID %>" data-product-pointer="<%= iPointer %>">
                   <table class="table table-condensed">
                     <tr>
                       <td class="r-condensed" style="color:red;"><small>Kat.</small></td><td class="r-condensed" style="color:red;"><small>Kat.</small></td><td class="r-condensed" style="color:red;"><small>BestNr.</small></td><td class="r-condensed" style="color:red;"><small>Preis</small></td>
                     </tr>
                     <% print(listItem.baskets); %>
                   </table>
                 </div>
                 <div class="tab-pane" id="basket-text-<%= listItem.skuID %>">
                   <div class="r-condensed" style="text-align: justify;width:100%;"><%= listItem.text %></div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="tab-pane" id="basket-picture-<%= listItem.skuID %>" data-product-image-url="client/bridgeland/img/<%= listItem.skuID %>.jpg">
                   <div class="media">
                     <a class="media-left" href="#">
                       <img class="media-object product-image" data-product-image-url="client/bridgeland/img/<%= listItem.skuID %>.jpg" data-src="" alt="Generic placeholder image">

               <!-- /Tab panes -->

    window.jQuery || document.write('<script src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-2.2.3.min.js"><\/script>')
   </script>
   <script src="vendor/tether.min.js">

   <script src="vendor/select2.full.min.js">
   </script>

   </script>
   <script src="vendor/jquery.typeahead.min.js">
   </script>
   <script src="vendor/jquery.toaster.js">
   </script>
   <script src="client/bridgeland/bridgeland.min.js">
   </script>
   <script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
         responsive();
         windowResize();
         try {
           var basketdb = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("basketCache"));
           var jsondb = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("dataCache"));
           var insqlArray = basketdb.dataSku;
           var data = [
             { id: 'Placeholder', text: 'Bitte eine Option wählen ...'},
             { id: 'Bridge-Bedarf', text: 'Bridge-Bedarf', children: [] },
             { id: 'Bridge-Boutique', text: 'Bridge-Boutique', children: [] },
             { id: 'Dekorative Karten', text: 'Bridge-Boutique', children: [] },
             { id: 'Bridge-Software', text: 'Bridge-Software', children: [] },
             { id: 'Bridge-Books', text: 'Bridge-Bücher', children: [] },
             { id: 'Bridge-Training', text: 'Bridge-Training', children: [] }
           ];
           data.forEach(function(el) {
             searchTerm = el.id;
             jsondb.forEach(function(element, index) {
                 if (element.dir == searchTerm) {
                   var obj = {'id':element.sku, 'text':element.name};
                   return el.children.push(obj);
                 }
             });
           });
           var $eventSelect = $(".js-example-data-array");
           $(".js-example-data-array").select2({
             data: data
           });
           $eventSelect.on("select2:select", function (e) {
             var searchTerm = $eventSelect.select2().val();
             searchAndAppendProducts(searchTerm, "sku");
           });
         } catch(e) {
           alert('Eine Version ohne lokale Datenbank gibt es bald.');
         }
         $.toaster({ settings : {'timeout':2000} });
         $.toaster('Willkommen im Bridgeland!', 'Bridgeland-Team', 'success');
     	});
   </script>
  </body>
